" shyaam benegal kamity kaa maananaa he ki board kaa kaam film ko certificate dene kaa hona chahie naa ki kanchi chalaane kaa
 It is better to be given a certificate of different status than to use scissors on the film
 isse filmkaar kii rachanaatmakataa bhi bani rahegi or board apana kaam bhi kar sakegaa
 The Benegal Committee has given its first report in four months
 report kaa aglaa or aakhri hissaa 20 june tak sarkaar ko saunp diya jayega
 The Censor Board Report, which does not operate arbitrary scissors, states that it should not be the job of the Board to arbitrarily censor films in the name of giving certificates
 film relies ho or apane mul rup main theatre tak pahunche, lekin uskaa certificate alag hoga or jaahir he ki darshak varg bhi
 Therefore, the Shyam Benegal Committee, in its report on the jurisdiction and functioning of the Central Board of Film Certification, has said these things in detail
 edlt vid coshan kaa ho alag certificatesuchana or prasaaran mantri arun jetali ko saunpi gai report main kamity ne saaf kaha he ki filmon koyu, yue or e certificatke maujuuda khaanche ke alaava ek do darje or badaye ja sakate hai
 But scissoring the creativity of the filmmaker is not appropriate
 edlt shrenee kii filmon ko or sakhti kaa certificate yani 'edlt vid coshan' kaa certificate diya ja saktaa he
 After all, we are in the new century
